Step 2 ^kSQWfWAe

Search Up returns nothing, set
position back to start. ^QpJ0n0V7

End ^LMoOxdtV

Step 3 ^ig7ZLPtn

Search Right returns nothing,
set position back to start.  ^hfoe3drH

Start ^9Cwm9f0w

End ^1qqvWtbJ

Step 4 ^bAiZL4mr

Search Down returns empty spot,
do another search from there.
This is where recursion kicks in. ^Z9Suv9tJ

Start ^4P5C2hMD

End ^NAYIzcN7

Step 5 ^Blcd2Kmr

Start has already been searched, skip. ^bgQYtYWP

Start ^akIIQQvX

End ^wrTPnqvH

Step 6 ^iCH2ExHA

Right returns nothing, go 
back to current position. ^Qh9F5DHb

Start ^IJjjDQ6l

End ^X0kQLNWJ

Step 7 ^mSGli1GJ

Search Down returns empty spot,
do another search from there. ^Z9eElDAG

Start ^wfmx0dGz

End ^UK8xXjIu

Step 7 ^fxiFuK4U

Search Down returns empty spot,
do another search from there. ^HhYS6yaB

I skipped the search
up, and right on this
one. ^jvG9ykxp

End ^n4lCJS7X

Step 8 ^kyzdhYpz

Dead end, remove all nodes
in this path from the result. ^EwsLUe6g

current path nodes = (4, 1), (4, 2), (4, 3) ^0NZXdkj6

current path nodes = (4, 0) ^oiv1Lmdq

current path nodes = (4, 0) ^AgisS9Iq

current path nodes = (4, 0), (4, 1), (4, 2), (4, 3) ^ORxz0p3m

Start ^BPUjeLHw

End ^CpWBbDMN

Step 9 ^aQwvhpfX

current path nodes = (4, 0), (4, 1), (4, 2) ^odnOSqkN

Back-trace 1, and search for any spots
not already included in the current path nodes.

Also, remove the previous node after the fact.

Be careful to do the removing AFTER searching 
for a slot that isn't included in current path
nodes.

You can do this by setting current node, equal 
to the second to last node in the current nodes,
and searching from there. 

This is easiest achieved by using the 'stack' data
structure, popping off the previous item as we go
 backwards in the path. ^xUuqsrD9

current node = (4, 0) ^Tb6u54Gw

current path nodes = (4, 0) ^RBFagdh5

current node = (4, 0) ^jNR8pubT

current path nodes = (4, 0) ^lJZ6F0XR

current node = (4, 0) ^3oveXKSM

current node = (4, 0) ^Rjj5UaCp

current path nodes = (4, 0), (4, 1) ^blHUGufn

current node = (4, 1) ^grKBNgLa

current path nodes = (4, 0), (4, 1) ^2MHW5wFD

current node = (4, 1) ^8VwNhTIk

current path nodes = (4, 0), (4, 1) ^levT6Hk8

current node = (4, 1) ^FFnOfLhj

current node = (4, 2) ^Pi5lvaAX

current node = (4, 3) ^z380qKcT

current node = (4, 2) ^xPgt4VDj

Start ^NfW05f0w

End ^NqJ9DBvZ

Step 10 ^HsL96Pa8

current path nodes = (4, 0), (4, 1) ^c6CMy156

current node = (4, 1) ^Z3mzfUmW

Now we found a new node that is not contained
in the list of all current path nodes, so we can
continue. ^Jdrb7Ov5
